The Future of Japanese Finance (Japanese Correspondence) 107

Rural Poverty, Increasing National Debt

The crisis in Japan's social economy in the 1934 settlement, such as the frost disaster in the six northeastern prefectures and the drought in Kyushu, has passed. However, the real difficulties will begin in 1935. The problem of not having enough to eat will affect the entire society and will gradually become apparent after the New Year. The military has distributed hundreds of thousands of pieces of clothing and other manufactured goods to local women in the area last winter, employing them in manual labor. The total number is indeed quite large, but it is very limited when divided. The fundamental problem in Japanese rural areas is not temporary but permanent. Therefore, people on both extremes have their own active proposals and express dissatisfaction with the current system.

Politically, at the end of last year, the abolition of the principle of ratio stipulated in the naval treaty was announced. Fortunately, it did not cause any unexpected repercussions internationally. From a certain perspective, it seems to be very beneficial. However, Britain's vigilance in naval bases such as Singapore and Hong Kong is quite obvious. Japan has hinted at concessions to Britain in order to seek future maneuverability, and even hopes for the revival of the Anglo-Japanese alliance. The United States has increased its military budget from US$585 million this year to US$792 million next year, plus US$100 million for reconstruction, bringing the total cost of the army and navy to US$900 million. Compared with Japan's 102.1 million, it is also evenly matched. Although Japan is outwardly very calm about this, it cannot but have some concerns and must quickly plan a response, which is all economically related.

In general economic terms, Japan seemed to have a lot of optimistic material in the past year. Steel production is expected to be around 3.9 million tons, which proves the rapid development of its military industry. In the event of an emergency, it is quite possible to be self-sufficient. In terms of export trade, cotton cloth alone is nearly 240 million square yards, and other artificial silks are all improving, creating a new record for her trade. The first regret is the decline in raw silk exports, which is less than half of the peak period. Oil production only totals 6 million boxes, which is only one-tenth of the total demand. Furthermore, due to the decline in raw silk prices, rural debt cannot be repaid at all, which has a huge impact on cities.

Therefore, although optimistic arguments about government finances are sung to the skies, pessimistic undercurrents are still surging. Although the general accounting revenue for the 1935 fiscal year has increased slightly, deficit bonds still need to be issued for 565 million yen. In addition, there are also special accounting and various business bonds, totaling 750 million yen. If these bonds are calculated at 4% interest, the interest on public debt will increase by at least 30 million yen next year. The various interest payments due before this year have been calculated to reach 37.8 million yen. Adding the aforementioned number, the interest to be paid after next year will be 480 million yen. As for the total amount of various bonds issued in the past, it was 864.1 million yen by the end of last year. Adding the 400 million yen that should have been issued in last year's budget but was not, and the bonds for the 1935 fiscal year, Japan's national debt will reach 987.7 million yen next year. There are also short-term national debts such as rice certificates and treasury securities, totaling more than 300 million yen. In total, it will exceed 1 billion yen. If the interest is calculated at 4%, it will be 400 million yen per year, accounting for one-fifth of Japan's total treasury expenditure, and more than one-half of tax revenue. The total amount accounts for almost one-tenth of Japan's total.

In this situation, who can say that Japan's financial strength is absolutely worry-free and always optimistic? When Takahashi Korekiyo came to power, he thought that there were many optimistic materials for the financial future, and that continuing to issue bonds would not be a problem because there was a market. Capitalists have more surplus power and are not at ease investing their surplus funds overseas. Buying public debt is more convenient. However, the changes in the world situation and the true peace are still unreliable. The expansion of armaments is natural. Japan's expansion of military spending is inevitable. Facing the so-called "international crisis," I am afraid that military spending will increase even more in the recent years, and how much more the number of public bonds will increase is currently difficult to predict. (January 28th in Tokyo)

The Solution of the Chahar Eastern Incident 108

Datatan Meeting was Simple in Form

Japanese Troops Withdrew and Firearms were Returned

Order Restored and Local Authorities Prepared Relief Work Beijing Correspondence: The Chahar Eastern issue, which both sides considered a misunderstanding, was resolved through several consultations and negotiations in Beijing. On the 2nd, a simple form was held in Datatan to resolve it on the spot, and it has now been completely concluded. The details of the process are recorded as follows:

Meeting Situation 109

After both parties decided on the meeting location and date, Zhang Yueting, Chief of Staff of the 37th Division on our side, arrived in Guyuan on the 1st. The Japanese side sent Matsui, a military liaison officer stationed in Zhangjiakou, to Guyuan to meet with Zhang. On the morning of the 2nd, Zhang led his entourage, Guo Yukai, Magistrate of Guyuan County, and Zhang Zude, Section Chief of the Chahar Provincial Government, along with Matsui to Datatan. They arrived at 11:00 AM. The Japanese military headquarters sent more than 20 soldiers to welcome them. They went to the Japanese military headquarters to meet with the Japanese representatives, Tanimitsu Isao and Nagami Toshiyoshi, and held a simple ceremony. In addition to expressing regret, they orally agreed on the solution, which was limited to military matters and did not mention politics. The meeting lasted only a few tens of minutes. At 12:00, they had lunch together at the headquarters. After the meal, Zhang and others left Datatan and returned to Zhangjiakou. At 8:15 AM on the morning of the 3rd, Zhang and Zhang Zude went to Beijing to report to He Yingqin and Song Zheyuan.

Solution 110

The solution is divided into four items as follows: 1. Express regret. 2. Guarantee that no unfortunate incidents will occur between the two parties in the future. 3. The line of Youtouchengzi, Nan Shizhuzi, and Dongzhaizi will be the boundary, and neither party will encroach on each other. 4. Return the firearms and ammunition seized from the Rehe militia. The military branch announced the solution on the 4th. The original text is recorded below: "According to the report of Song Zheyuan, Commander of the 29th Army and Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Government, regarding the Chahar Eastern incident, Zhang Yueting, Chief of Staff of the 37th Division of the 29th Army, was sent to Datatan on February 2nd with his entourage Guo Yukai, Magistrate of Guyuan County, and Zhang Zude, Section Chief of the Chahar Provincial Government, to meet with Tanimitsu Isao, Commander of the 13th Brigade of the 7th Division of the Japanese Army, Nagami Toshiyoshi, Commander of the 25th Regiment, and Matsui in Saza. They reached an oral agreement on the solution at 11:00 AM that morning. The Chahar Eastern incident originated from a misunderstanding. Now, in order to peacefully resolve the situation, the Japanese army will immediately return to its original defense, and the 29th Army will not intrude into the line of Shitouchengzi, Nan Shizhuzi, and Dongzhaizi, and the area to its east. All the rifles (37 in total) and 1,500 rounds of ammunition seized by the 29th Army from the Rehe militia will be delivered to Datatan by the Magistrate of Guyuan County on the 7th of this month for return to the Rehe militia."

Japanese Troops Withdraw 111

After the agreement was reached by both parties, the Japanese army began to withdraw on the 3rd. The 25th Regiment stationed in Shitouchengzi, Nantan, and other places was withdrawn to its original defense at Gubeikou. The withdrawal has now been completed. The 37 rifles and 1,500 rounds of ammunition seized by our side from the Rehe militia will also be sent to the Japanese military headquarters in Datatan this afternoon (7th).

Order Restored 112

After the Japanese army withdrew, Changliang, Wunihe, Nanbei Shizhuzi, Sidaogou, Mingshatan, and Dongzhaizi were maintained by security police and militia, and order was restored. The Chahar provincial authorities, in view of the fact that the Japanese army invaded eastern Chahar, shelled Dongzhaizi, and sent planes to drop bombs in Dushikou and other places, causing casualties among residents, and destroying houses by bombing, resulting in extremely heavy losses, ordered the provincial government to send personnel to investigate and provide relief to various places, and handle the aftermath. (7th)

Inauguration of the Gan Province Pacification Conference 113

Discussing Matters Related to Suppression, Post-Disaster Recovery, and Rejuvenation

All Pacification Commanders, Commissioners, and Others Attended

Nanchang Correspondence: Gu Zhutong, Director of Jiangxi Pacification, in order to swiftly eliminate remnant bandits, stabilize the region, restore vitality, and plan for rejuvenation, specially convened a provincial pacification conference. It opened on the morning of the sixth at 9:00 AM at the headquarters. Attendees included Pacification Director Gu Zhutong, Chief of Staff Han Deqin, Provincial Chairman Xiong Shihui, various Route Commanders such as Fan Songfu, Pacification Zone Commanders Zhao Guantao, Chen Jicheng, Mao Bingwen, Liu Xing, Zhang Fang, Sun Lianzhong, Tan Daoyuan, Third Route Deputy Commander Luo Zhuoying, Administrative Commissioners and Concurrently Security Commanders Lin Jing, Fan Suzhong, Cao Zubin, Mo Xiong, Hua Xi, Guo Su, Zhou Zuofu, Zhang Dulun, Wang Youlan, Li Zhengyi, Zhang Chi, Shao Hongji, and over sixty senior officials from the Security Office and Pacification Headquarters. Chairman Gu Zhutong presided over the opening ceremony as customary. Gu delivered an opening speech, roughly stating, "This conference aims to establish practical pacification plans, coordinate steps between the Party, government, and military, advance together unanimously, swiftly eliminate remnant bandits, and seek the region's rejuvenation. I hope everyone will strive to fulfill the duties of suppression, post-disaster recovery, stabilization, and rejuvenation." This was followed by a speech from Xiong Shihui, mostly containing words of encouragement. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM and resumed at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. The heads of the military and political groups of the proposal review committee reported on the proposal review opinions and summarized the methods, followed by discussions. Many decisions were made regarding military affairs, transportation, management, health, justice and security, and other matters. On the seventh, discussions continued on political post-disaster recovery cases. The conference is scheduled to last approximately three days.

Xiong Shihui, with the commissioners and security commanders of various regions gathered in Nanchang, convened a meeting at the provincial government yesterday. The commissioners reported on the political and suppression situation in their respective jurisdictions, and many instructions were given for improving the difficulties in each region's work. The commissioners also exchanged opinions and corrected each other's mistakes.

The Provincial Anti-Banditry Association is scheduled to host a banquet for Director Gu and all members of the Pacification Conference at the YMCA on the seventh, with all members of the Provincial Party Department and Provincial Government as guests, to offer comfort and appreciation. (February 6th)

Liu Zhenhua Goes to Xunyang 114

Reporting on the Suppression of Anhui Bandits

Wuhu Correspondence: Anhui Chairman Liu Zhenhua, accompanied by Secretary Chen Shikai and guards, departed for Wuhu in seven or eight cars of various sizes at 5:00 PM today from the Shuntunxi Administrative Office. He is temporarily staying at the Dahua Hotel. According to what he said to visitors, his sole purpose in governing during these difficult times for the people is to ensure that they are "poor but at peace." Only when the people can live peacefully can other matters be discussed. Therefore, he will devote all his efforts to suppressing bandits. After the Anhui bandits caused disturbances, he immediately went to Tunxi with key members of the provincial government to supervise the suppression. Now, the bandit leader has been captured and the bandit forces have been completely eliminated. Not counting those who escaped, as many as four thousand bandits were captured, and nearly three thousand guns were seized. The order of Anhui is now completely restored, with dense fortifications and further progress in transportation construction. The Tunxi-Jingdezhen and Xiuning-Qimen sections of the road have been built within a limited time. The road surface project was completed and opened to traffic on the first day of the Lunar New Year. He personally went to inspect the road. Many villagers have returned home to live peacefully. Anhui tea is a specialty of Anhui Province, with an annual sales value of over 20 million yuan. Tea farmers occupy an important position in rural areas. Spring is the season for planting tea. This time, Anhui was severely ravaged by bandits. If the tea farmers are prevented from planting and doing business, the loss will be even greater. Compared to raising funds for temporary disaster relief, the work is immeasurable. Therefore, after the complete restoration of order in Anhui, he deeply hopes that domestic financial and industrial circles and Anhui natives living abroad will invest and lend money, and not miss this greatest source of profit. This is also an essential plan for the revitalization of rural southern Anhui. He plans to rush to Lushan on the eighth, but because the Yangtze River steamer had already departed, he had to stay overnight and take the Yangtze River steamer upstream tomorrow. After finishing matters in Xunyang, he will return to Anqing to handle government affairs, and then go to Tunxi again. In addition to supervising the cleaning of the countryside, he will devote more effort to tea farmers in the spring to seek revitalization. (February 6th)

Surrendered Bandits and Civilians in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Area Urgently Need Relief 115

Luotian Dispatch: In recent months, the Red Bandits in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have suffered repeated heavy blows, and their main forces have been routed. The remaining bandits, after being suppressed and pacified by the National Army, have surrendered with their weapons and reformed themselves. However, the internal situation of the bandits has long been dire, and their lives have been entirely dependent on looting. Once they surrender, they lack food and clothing. Moreover, the civilians in the Red areas have repeatedly suffered from banditry and have long been displaced, with most homes empty. In this severe winter, with wind and snow, the surrendered bandits and disaster victims in the Red areas have no clothing or food, and their cries of hunger and cold are particularly distressing. It is reported that Liang Guanying, Commander-in-Chief of the Twenty-Fifth Route Army, witnessed the tragic situation and was deeply moved by compassion. He believes that without effective relief, the situation cannot be completely cleared. In addition to drawing over three thousand sets of old cotton military uniforms, which were converted into relief clothing with the words "Relief Clothing" printed to distinguish them from military uniforms, Liang also led the officers and soldiers of the army to make voluntary donations to establish an emergency relief association for assistance. Liang also recently appealed to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, Deputy Commander Zhang, and sent telegrams to the governments of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui to appeal for disaster relief and raise funds for proper relief. It is reported that the Wuhan Three Provinces Anti-Banditry Headquarters plans to allocate several thousand yuan per month, and Anhui Chairman Liu Zhenhua has already allocated three thousand yuan, which will be distributed by Liang. The scope of relief is limited to surrendered refugees and genuinely starving people in the area. Since the implementation, the number of surrendered bandits has been increasing, and the starving people in the disaster area also hope to obtain warmth and food and get through this severe winter. Judging from the current situation, the complete suppression of the Red Bandits in the area is not far away.

Songjiang

Changqiao Elementary School Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition 116

Changqiao Town, located in the eastern part of Songjiang County, has always had an elementary school. Its scale is small, and its equipment is simple. It urgently needs to be expanded. A certain gentleman in the town, enthusiastic about education, generously took the responsibility of building a school building. He engaged in fundraising, reaching as far as Beijing and Shanghai, and as far as overseas, raising over five thousand yuan. Construction began and was completed in half a year, and the content began to be gradually improved. Shen Jingquan, the principal of the school, and teachers Gu Mingde, Ji Zongwei, Jiang Fuzhen, and others are all able to patiently guide students. At the beginning of this semester, there were many students, and the classrooms could not accommodate them. The gentleman planned to build more school buildings. He obtained three hundred pieces of calligraphy and painting from contemporary celebrities. From the fourth to the tenth of this month, an exhibition was held at the New Songjiang Society on Songhui Road in Songjiang, and the works were priced for sale, with the proceeds used to expand the school buildings. The reporter happened to visit the society and felt that it was full of dazzling and beautiful works. Among them were Liu San's clerical script, Lu Weizhao's running script, Yang Qianli's cursive script, Wang Zhilin's landscape and running script, Fei Longding's seal script, Zhang Zuocheng's landscape, Yu Jifan's flowers, Lou Yuqing's birds and animals, Yu Xiaolian's animals, Tang Yifang's figures, and Li Zhongjie, Huang Zongxiang, and Zhang Xiaoshi's figure landscapes, all of which are rare artistic masterpieces, and the prices are very low. The reporter spent five yuan to buy a couplet by Liu San, which was very satisfactory. Those who have a fondness for calligraphy and painting should not miss it.

General Situation of Various Industries 117

This county relies mainly on agricultural products, and the prosperity of commerce depends on the abundance of agricultural harvests. Last summer was a severe drought, which greatly affected the rural areas. Fortunately, there was continuous rainfall in the autumn, and the autumn harvest was celebrated. Moreover, the price of rice was high, and the market saw a turnaround. Compared to previous years, it was very different, and the farmers were also very happy. The general business situation of various industries last year is surveyed as follows: Finance Industry, Pawn Industry: Banks and Farmers' Banks have surpluses, and the performance of warehousing is also good. However, the Xingye Branch was affected by the Shanghai branch and has already closed down. It is currently being sued by creditors. After the Money Shop industry has been steadily lending, they all have surpluses. It is reported that Xinyu Ying has a surplus of 10,000 yuan, and Sheng Yuan Cheng Da has a surplus of 8,000 yuan each, and Yu Kang also has a surplus of 5,000 yuan, making it the most promising business in Songshi. The Rice Industry has surpluses due to the continued rise in rice prices. Other industries such as oil, sesame, paint, wheat bran, second-hand clothing, and sundries also have surpluses. The silk and cloth industry has only the Meili Company on Malu Bridge with a surplus, while the rest are average. The industry's thread blankets and cloth factories are all sluggish in sales and have not seen a good situation. Foreign goods and medicinal materials have suffered slight losses, while tea, wine, and local goods are average. The wood industry has a surplus, while the rest are average. However, Shangyi Foreign Goods Store and Qia Daxi Silk and Cloth Store did not welcome the god of wealth last night and seem to be on the verge of closing down.

Wuxi 122

Five Counties' Rice Industry Changes to New Measuring Instruments

The peck used by the rice industry in this county was different in size during the Qing Guangxu years. In the first year of Xuantong, the Cao peck was uniformly used and calibrated for use every year. Last year, the rice industry was ordered to change to new measuring instruments, which could not be implemented due to lack of resources. Now, the rice industry in Wuxi, Wujin, Kunshan, Wu County, and Wujiang has changed to new measuring instruments yesterday (8th) to comply with the orders. According to the official peck regulations, the mouth is narrow and the bottom is wide, starting from Jia Sidao of the Song Dynasty. During the Zhiyuan period of the Yuan Dynasty, Zhongcheng Cui or Yan said that the style was narrow at the mouth and wide at the bottom, so the income and expenditure were not very different, and it was implemented in the world. After a long time, the practice was used without modification. The small mouth of the peck means that the peck surface may be shallow or full, and the income and expenditure are limited. Therefore, the method of preventing fraud is very good. Although Jia was a treacherous minister, this regulation of one thing is beneficial to the world.

Changshu 123

Road Construction Workers Cause Trouble

Suspension of Sochang Ship

The workers of the Changhua Company, which is building the Suchang Highway, are mostly from other places. Because they have repeatedly obstructed the Suchang ships to and from each other, they have aroused the suspension of the Suchang route by all the ship bureaus, which has lasted for four days and has not been resolved. Transportation has been greatly affected, and mail has also been delayed. According to the occurrence of this incident, the Zhongban ship of the Huitong Company returned to Changzhou from Suzhou on the 3rd. When passing near Wuta Town, dozens of road construction workers forcibly detained the ship and forced it to tow heavy objects. The ship bureau refused to tow because it was afraid of delaying time, which led to a conflict. The workers injured Jin Hongzhi, the cashier of the accounting office. That night, they went to the county government to examine the injury. The next morning, they agreed to recruit merchants, Huimin, Lao Gongmao, and ship bureaus to suspend navigation together. Since then, transportation between Suzhou and Changzhou has been cut off. The county government, fearing the expansion of the situation, sent personnel to mediate. Now the ship bureau has put forward four requirements: 1. Road construction workers can buy half-price tickets to take a boat with a certificate. 2. Refuse to tow heavy materials. If there is an empty boat, it will also be towed at half price. 3. The above two methods shall be handled by the county's letter to the engineering office, and shall be acknowledged in writing by the company. In the future, workers who have the courage to rely on should be investigated according to law. 4. Arrest and investigate the murderers who caused the incident. There are also additional actions, requesting to send more security team members to protect the ship in the most recent ten days. The county government accepted all of them, but the attachment was postponed because the number of team members was insufficient. Now the conditions are roughly appropriate, and there is a saying that the shipping will resume on the ninth.

Letter from Songjiang Electric Company 125

Respectfully, I read in the local news column of the 8th of your newspaper, "All the telephones in the Songjiang city were damaged." This does not quite match the facts. It was found that on the 6th, Songjiang was hit by wind and snow, and several telephone poles were broken and touched the low-voltage wires of the electric lights. At that time, the telephone company called to notify us, but the meaning was unclear and the call was interrupted. We immediately sent workers to rush to the scene and learned that the company had cut off the main line. At the same time, our company sent the entire team of craftsmen to help investigate. Upon re-examination the next day, it was found that there were as many as nine breaks, which have been reported to the company for repair. This is the process of the situation. I am deeply afraid that the outside world does not know the truth and misunderstandings occur, so I specially write to inform you. I hope you will make corrections. This is addressed to the chief writer of Shen Bao, Songjiang Electric Co., Ltd. (February 8th)

Financial Advisory Committee Established Today 126

The Ministry of Finance's Financial Advisory Committee has appointed Li Fusun, Chen Guangfu, Bei Songsun, Xi Demao, Song Ziliang, Tang Shoumin, Zhou Zuomin, Wu Daquan, Hu Bijiang, Qian Xinzhi, Qin Runqing, Zhang Gongquan, Xu Xinliu, and Qian Changzhao as members. The eleven articles of the committee's charter have been announced by the Ministry of Finance and printed for distribution to the members for their reference. The committee is divided into four groups: the first group studies and improves the current monetary situation; the second group studies and stabilizes exchange rates; the third group studies and improves international receipts and payments; and the fourth group studies and regulates domestic financial matters. In addition to the provision that the chairman will be the president of the Central Bank, today's meeting will elect a vice chairman, a director of each group, and the distribution of duties of each member.

The Haili Has Not Been Robbed 131

Arrived in Shanghai on the 6th, Now Sailing to Qingdao

Various Rumors Are Groundless

Central News Agency reports: Since the Taikoo Steamship Company's Tongzhou ship was robbed by pirates, all sea vessels have stepped up their defenses to prevent accidents. Suddenly, there were rumors that the China Merchants Bureau's Haili ship also encountered pirates. A Central News Agency reporter made a special trip to inquire about everything at the bureau. According to the person in charge of the bureau, since the Puan ship was robbed, the bureau's ships operating along the coast have increased the number of navigation police and added anti-theft equipment to prevent accidents. Therefore, no accidents have occurred since then. After the robbery of the Taikoo Steamship Company's Tongzhou ship, the bureau's sea vessels will be extra vigilant to ensure safe voyages. The reporter then inquired about the rumors of the Haili ship encountering pirates. It was said that when the Haili ship was sailing between Shantou and Hong Kong, it was already night. The patrolling navigation police suddenly faintly saw someone climbing up the "Wind Turbine." They immediately rushed to investigate, but the person was gone. The entire navigation police were notified to be on alert and searched the cabins, but no suspicious person or robbery was found. The order was good, and no incident occurred at all. The ship returned to Shanghai on the 6th and will sail north to Qingdao on the 9th.

British Parliament Continues to Discuss the Tongzhou Ship Robbery Case 132

Masden's Question

Caused Laughter

Reuters, London, 7th: At today's meeting of the House of Commons, the Tongzhou ship robbery was mentioned again. Conservative MP Agnew proposed that the British Ambassador to China, Kadgan, be instructed to negotiate with the Chinese government to clear the pirate dens in Dapeng Bay and other places with the assistance of the British Navy. Secretary of State Eden replied that the problem of pirates in Chinese waters is currently being carefully considered. All plans that can help this matter will not be ignored. The Chinese and British navies are currently cooperating closely. It is not beneficial to continue other actions at this time. The MP also said that he heard that this kind of pirate cannot be eradicated by the navy alone. Eden replied that he thought that the actions taken at sea had achieved particularly good results. Eden continued that the British Consul General in Shanghai, Bilinan, will, together with the naval authorities and the Shanghai Municipal Council's Police Department, thoroughly investigate the robbery of the Tongzhou ship. Agnew then asked the government whether it intended to ask the Chinese government to send troops to besiege the pirates' dens on the shore. Eden replied that the close cooperation between the Chinese and British authorities was very effective. Then Conservative MP Masden asked Eden whether he would ask the League of Nations to convey the pirates to show goodwill, which caused laughter. Eden did not answer.

Everything said must be translated into English, so it will take some time. It is said that experts will be consulted to revise the anti-theft measures, with particular emphasis on the ship passenger regulations, iron fences, and radio.

Yangtze River Water Level Suddenly Drops, "Jiang Hua" Ship Aground at Huangzhou 134

Freed After a Day and Night of Unloading Cargo

Large Yangtze River Vessels Suspended

Since November 15th of last year, the water volume of the upper Yangtze River has been steadily increasing, with the gauge between Hankou and Jiujiang consistently at 16 feet 5 inches, and between Jiujiang and Wuhu consistently at 18 feet 6 inches. These levels are rarely seen in historical water gauge records. Therefore, even during the dry winter season, large, shallow-draft ships could navigate. Companies did not increase their shallow-draft fees, assuming there would be no receding of the Yangtze River. However, after the beginning of spring, the upper river water level dropped dramatically, with decreases of over four feet in a single day. Yesterday, various shipping companies received reports from Hankou stating that the water level had dropped sharply since the afternoon of the 6th. The level between Hankou and Xunyang had fallen to 11 feet 2 inches, and between Xunyang and Wuhu to only 12 feet 3 inches. The water is expected to continue receding on the 7th and 8th. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River vessel "Jiang Hua" left Shanghai for Hankou on the 5th of this month. When it sailed upriver from Shanghai, the upper river water level had not yet dropped significantly, only gradually decreasing. On the morning of the 7th, when the ship reached the Huangzhou section of the river above Jiujiang, the water gauge suddenly decreased. The "Jiang Hua" ship, with its deeper draft, ran aground. Ship numbers 24214, 2 award 41214, 3 award 10218, awarded scholarships to 35 students by Yu Guang School in Shude Lane, Xinzha Road. The following awards will be presented by participating manufacturers, and the last four characters will receive a copy of the Yu Guang weekly calendar.

All Businesses Reopened Yesterday 135

However, Vacant Properties for Rent Are Conspicuous

Shanghai's banks, money shops, exchanges, and stores of all sizes resumed business yesterday after a four-day spring festival holiday that began on the 4th. However, the market economy remains as depressed as before, and the number of "For Rent" signs on buildings along the streets is strikingly high, almost unprecedented for such a dismal economic situation in Shanghai.

Owner Chen Jin Yu, assumed it could free itself, so he immediately reversed the engine, planning to leave the shallows. Unexpectedly, the bottom of the ship sank deeply into the shallow sand, and could not move. Owner Chen had no choice but to telegraph a report to the Shanghai General Bureau and ask for a ship to be sent for rescue. The General Bureau immediately telegraphed the Hankou Branch, ordering Branch Manager Cai Lisheng to quickly order the Jiang Jing vessel on its way to the Huangzhou river surface, to drag the Jiang Hua out. Later, according to a follow-up telegram, the Jiang Jing's efforts to tow the ship failed due to shallow waters. Furthermore, since the Jiang Hua could not be dragged out of the shallows due to the continuous decrease of water in the Hanxun section of the river, the Shanghai Bureau telegraphed Hankou again, ordering the dispatch of the Li Ji and Mei Li vessels, and to send workers from Hankou to unload the cargo and passengers from the Jiang Hua, in order to reduce the load and attempt to rescue it. On the 7th, throughout the day and night, part of the ship's cargo was unloaded in succession, carried back to Hankou by the Mei Li and other vessels. The Jiang Shun vessel was also ordered to Huangzhou to tow the ship. By 8:30 AM yesterday morning, the Jiang Hua vessel had been dragged out of the shallows. Yesterday afternoon, the Shanghai Bureau received a telegram stating that the Jiang Hua had been rescued and was now sailing to Hankou. The passengers on board had also safely arrived in Hankou, and the cargo was undamaged. Whether the bottom of the ship was damaged during the grounding will be inspected after its arrival in Shanghai.

A telegram from the Jianghan Customs notified Shanghai shipping companies that all vessels going up and down the river, starting yesterday, are restricted in their cargo loading draft, not to exceed 11 feet 2 inches. If this limit is exceeded, it will be difficult to reach Hankou. As a result, large vessels with a draft exceeding 12 feet in the Yangtze River have suspended operations. The Sanbei Changxing vessel, due to its large hull and draft of around 13 feet, was decided to be suspended and sent to the factory for repairs today. Other larger vessels from various companies have also reduced their cargo tonnage starting yesterday.

The original text is excerpted below. Regarding the request for four points to be adopted for this year's spring cocoon season. We respectfully submit that the cocoon industry is declining and nearing extinction. If it is not maintained, it will disappear. We have heard that the Department plans to implement control measures for this year's spring cocoon. The cocoon merchants are all in a state of anxiety due to their personal interests. In order to protect the interests of all Zhejiang cocoon merchants, the association convened a temporary meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members and representatives from the cocoon industry trade unions of various counties on January 29th. A unanimous resolution was passed to request four points, which are listed below. (1) Please exempt the cocoon improvement fee for this year's spring cocoon. (2) Regarding the purchase of native silkworm fresh cocoons, in addition to complying with the prices set by the official authorities, the rest should be free to operate. (3) In addition to the areas designated by the official authorities, the cocoon shops should be freely negotiated and leased by the cocoon merchants and shop owners. (4) Before the promulgation of the management methods for cocoon collection and control methods, the Department or the Silkworm Silk Control Committee should first submit a draft to the association for discussion, so that they can contribute their opinions. It is respectfully submitted that the above four points have been discussed repeatedly, so as to ensure that the government's great plan to improve silk cocoons does not disregard the cocoon merchants' last resort for survival. The cocoon merchants' last chance for survival is just a thread. We respectfully request that the Department grant full adoption, so that in the midst of renewed governance, there is both compassion for merchants and convenience for the people. All Zhejiang cocoon merchants await respite. Respectfully submitted by Zeng, Director of the Zhejiang Construction Department.

All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Conference Decides to Continue Spring Relief Efforts 144

Continue Donating 200,000 Yuan

Publish Donation Appeal

According to the Public News Agency, the Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association decided to continue with spring relief efforts, as the winter relief efforts had concluded, but the relief grain distributed was very small and the disaster victims could not maintain their livelihoods. A joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees was held at 3:00 PM yesterday to discuss solutions. More than 20 people attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Chu Huiseng, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Shen Junru, Zhang Shenzhi, Wu Zhihao, Mao Heyuan, and Cha Zhongjian. It was decided to continue spring relief efforts to help the disaster victims. The details are as follows:

Continue Spring Relief: Chairman Chu Huiseng first reported on the income and expenditure figures, the situation of the winter relief efforts, and the letters and telegrams requesting relief from various parties. The following proposals were then decided: (1) Although the winter relief efforts have ended, the amount of relief grain distributed was very small. With the harvest still far off, the disaster victims cannot maintain their lives. Should we continue with spring relief efforts in order to thoroughly provide relief? It was decided to continue with spring relief efforts. In addition to requesting funds from the province, there is still a shortage of approximately 200,000 yuan. We should do our best to raise funds from all sectors of society, publish a thank-you note in the newspaper for the donors who donated before January 3rd, and publish a report on the association's winter relief efforts, as well as income, expenditure, and relief summaries. (2) To send Chu Huiseng, Wang Xiaolai, and Zhang Xiaolin to Hangzhou on behalf of the association to request funds from the province in order to facilitate the continuation of spring relief efforts. It was decided to approve this proposal. (3) The deadline for spring relief is approaching, and the association should intensify its work and set 5:00 PM every day as the time for all committee members to attend meetings and discuss matters in order to facilitate progress. It was decided to approve this proposal. Rest omitted.

Donation Appeal: The Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association issued a donation appeal to report on the progress of the winter relief efforts and to continue with the spring relief efforts. We respectfully inform you that last year's drought in Zhejiang Province affected almost the entire province. More than 50 counties experienced harvests of 20% or less, and millions of disaster victims were without clothes or food, and died daily. This association witnessed this heartbreaking situation and solicited donations to provide relief. Since the start of the efforts, we have raised more than 148,000 yuan. At this time of social and economic hardship, we deeply rely on the enthusiastic contributions of all great philanthropists to achieve such results and to revive those on the brink of death. On behalf of the disaster victims, we express our deepest gratitude. However, there are too many disaster victims, and our efforts to provide widespread relief are hampered by limited resources. After consulting with the Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association and the Shanghai Fundraising for Provincial Drought Relief Association, we agreed to divide the responsibilities. The Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association is responsible for 22 counties, and the Drought Relief Association is responsible for 12 counties. This association is responsible for 13 counties, and we have followed the principle of providing relief grain to those who cannot survive without it, focusing on the elderly, weak, women, and children. We have distributed winter relief, allocating all the donated funds and the 50,000 yuan allocated by the Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association. We distributed 8,000 bags of relief powder in Jiaxing, 8,000 bags of relief powder in Chongde, 6,000 bags of relief powder in Tongxiang, 1,000 shi of relief rice in each of the three counties of Wukang, Yuhang, and Deqing, 5,000 dan of corn and 1,700 shi of relief rice in the three counties of Shangyu, Xinchang, and Shengxian, 2,000 shi of relief rice in Haiyan, and more than 2,000 yuan each for relief rice in parts of Shaoxing and Yuyao. Each county has been carefully assigned a relief director, who strictly investigates without omission or abuse, and the county governments have received the relief grain and distributed it to the disaster victims in person. In Haining County, the relief efforts were carried out by the Chinese Health Association, the Red Cross Society, and the Bodhi Dharma Association, with 5,000 yuan allocated by this association. This association also subsidized 4,000 yuan each to the two counties of Wuxing and Shouchang. This is a general overview of the winter relief efforts. Detailed accounts will be published after completion to ensure transparency. The winter relief grain distributed only provided enough porridge for an average of one month per person due to limited funds and widespread disaster. From the time of distribution until the beginning of spring, the small amount of relief grain received has been exhausted. With the harvest still far off and spring planting remote, the future is dire, and lives are at risk. If spring relief efforts are not continued, these tens of thousands of elderly, weak, women, and children will inevitably end up in ditches. This association fears that the relief efforts will not be thorough and will abandon previous efforts, burdening the great philanthropists' merits. We have no choice but to continue with spring relief efforts to fulfill our responsibility. We estimate that we need to raise approximately 200,000 yuan. We respectfully request that all domestic dignitaries and ladies of the boudoir generously open their purses and contribute generously. Those who have already donated are requested to donate more to complete the effort, and those who have not yet donated are requested to donate quickly to sow the seeds of virtue. We await your contributions with utmost anticipation. Respectfully yours.

Jianghai Customs Proclamation on Shipping Package Weight Regulations 146

Jianghai Customs issued Proclamation No. 1427 yesterday, stating that it had received an order from the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance to issue regulations on marking the weight of shipping packages and to strictly comply with them. Therefore, we must comply. The aforementioned regulations are now copied below: Article 1: All packages or items transported by sea or inland river, with a total weight of more than 1,000 kilograms, must have their weight marked on the packages or items by the sender before boarding the ship. The aforementioned markings can be made with labels, no less than four square inches wide and six square inches long. The material should be durable, the lettering should be clear, and the attachment to the package or item should be firm. Article 2: The text on the labels must be in Chinese characters and Arabic numerals. For packages or items imported from abroad, if the text on the labels is originally in a foreign language, the customs shall translate it into Chinese. Article 3: In the case of huge timber, heavy iron and stone, and other similar items, where it is impossible to determine the exact weight due to special circumstances, the sender shall mark the approximate weight in accordance with the provisions of Article 1. Article 4: If the weight of a package or item is not marked, the ship owner or its representative shall report the approximate weight of each item to the stevedores during unloading. Article 5: If the sender is a legal person or lacks capacity for civil conduct, the responsibilities stipulated in these regulations shall be borne by the legal person's representative or their legal representative. Article 6: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation. All merchants are hereby notified.

Yi Fangshuo's Appeal Case 159

The Debate Concluded Yesterday

Bail Granted Pending Ruling

Yi Fangshuo, a comedian from Hangzhou who performed in the rooftop garden of the New-New Company, was arrested by the French Concession police after being accused of raping his cousin Yi Baozhu. It was also found that Yi bought women Ye Jinzhu and Yang Lingzhu at a price, made them learn drama, and monitored their actions. He was transferred to the Second Special Court and prosecuted on three charges: obscenity, harming the family, and restricting freedom. During the trial, the plaintiff withdrew the charge of obscenity. As a result of the trial, he was sentenced to three years in prison only for the charge of restricting freedom. He was found not guilty of harming the family, and the charge of obscenity was not accepted. Yi refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court, based on the complaint, scheduled a hearing yesterday afternoon to summon witnesses. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday morning, Yi's guarantor, surnamed Weng, was summoned to court for questioning. At 1:00 PM, the witnesses in the case, Yi Baozhu, Li Xiaozhen, Ye Jinzhu, and Yang Lingzhu, and Yang Yi (Yang Lingzhu's mother-in-law, Yi Fangshuo's sister) and Ye Li (Ye Jinzhu's mother) arrived at the court to await questioning. At 3:00 PM, Judge Guo Dezhang, together with Judges Sun Honglin and Jia Gen, and Clerk Huang Lixiang, together with Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, opened the third criminal court for trial. Lawyer Yuan Jiahuang represented the Public Security Office in court. The appellant was defended by lawyers Sha Xunyi and Lou Yunmei. This case caused a sensation in society and attracted a large crowd of onlookers to the court yesterday. After the court opened, the officials ordered the bailiffs to bring the appellant Yi Fangshuo from the detention center. They first asked his age, origin, address, and occupation, and then asked Yi about the case of restricting freedom. The First Instance Court of the Second Special District sentenced you to three years in prison. Are you appealing because you disagree? Yi replied yes. The officials ordered him to state the reasons for his disagreement. Yi replied that this was completely unjust. They were very free and easy to learn drama in my place. Their actions were not monitored. Moreover, they were all relatives and children who voluntarily learned drama. Those who wanted to learn for three to five years, and those who didn't want to would go back. There were no contracts or fixed terms. He was asked if they (referring to Yi Baozhu, Li Xiaozhen, Yang Lingzhu, and Ye Jinzhu) testified very clearly in the original trial that their actions were monitored by his wives and concubines. He replied no, it was really unjust. When they went to perform, they went with the performers. Their performances were in front, and my wife was behind. My wives and concubines all performed with me, so how could they monitor them? However, after they gave a good performance, they were still accompanied home by the performers. He was asked if Yi Baozhu and Li Xiaozhen testified very clearly in the original trial that they were not allowed to go out alone and had to be accompanied by someone. Ye Jinzhu testified most clearly. He replied that it was unjust. He was asked if the two girls, Yang Lingzhu and Ye Jinzhu, were bought by him. He replied no. Yang Lingzhu was his nephew's wife, and Ye Jinzhu was the daughter of Section Chief Ye, who was introduced by a man named Zhou. Now Zhou has drowned. They verbally agreed to a three- to five-year term for learning drama. During the learning period, he was responsible for the teachers' salaries, food, and clothing. The income from the performances was also his. After they successfully learned, they would be given an uncertain amount of one to twenty yuan per period, and one yuan per hall for each performance. At this point, the officials summoned Yi Baozhu, Li Xiaozhen, Yang Lingzhu, and Ye Jinzhu to court and questioned them about monitoring and restricting freedom. The testimony of the four women completely overturned their testimony to the original trial and the police. They denied that anyone was monitoring them. They had never testified in the original trial or to the police that their actions were being monitored. Yang Yi testified that he brought Jian Chen to be his daughter-in-law. His son is twelve years old this year. Her original surname was Wang, and she entered the family at the age of six. Her father had died, and her mother's name was Wang Caiying, who had remarried and was now unknown. When she was brought into the family, he gave her a bellyache money of four yuan. Ye Li testified that Jinzhu was his daughter. She was born to his sister, who gave her to him as his daughter three months after his child died. On the 26th day of the tenth month of her tenth year, she was brought to Yi Fangshuo to learn drama through the introduction of a man named Zhou. At this point, the officials ordered the debate to begin. First, the prosecutor stated his opinion, and then the lawyer from the Public Security Office and the appellant's defense lawyer debated each other. The court announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict to be announced at 2:00 PM on the 15th. The appellant was still remanded to custody. Yi's defense lawyer requested that he be granted bail. The officials ordered that the decision be made after deliberation.

More Than Eighty Handcarts Confiscated 160

Increasing Numbers Without License Plates

Obstructing Traffic, All Confiscated

There is a type of handcart in Shanghai that is purely made of iron, with a rectangular body and four wheels on the bottom. One end of the cart is equipped with an iron rod, allowing it to be pushed by hand. This type of iron cart is almost a necessity for tobacco and paper shops and tofu shops, used to transport copper coins and tofu. It is common to see them on the streets. The Public Works Department Traffic Office has always considered them small in size and not affecting traffic on the roads. Therefore, any vehicle is required to have a license plate donated by the owner before it is allowed to be driven, but this type of cart is given preferential treatment, exempted from donating a license plate, and allowed to pass at will, without any restrictions or interference. Recently, they have been seen in increasing numbers. Those responsible for traffic management believe that since the creation of the license plate donation system has failed to cover them, and allowing them to continue to be let go will be even more detrimental to traffic, a notice has been issued to all police stations that if any such vehicles are found to be obstructing traffic, they should be taken to the police station for disposal in accordance with the law. In recent days, the number of carts detained by the Xinzha Police Station has reached as many as eighty. Yesterday, a large car was used to transport all the confiscated iron carts to the First Special District Local Court for disposal. After being questioned by the judge of the vehicle affairs court, it was ruled that all the vehicles should be confiscated. This is the first time that this type of cart has been confiscated.

Tan Dajinlong is Extremely Unscrupulous

Recently, he saw that Ms. Zhang was even more beautiful than before, but he could not touch her and was slapped instead, which made him angrier. He picked up a sharp little file at a certain wharf, and on the morning of the 31st of last month, at 6:45 AM, he secretly waited at the intersection of East Broadway Road and Huaji Road. When Ms. Zhang and her companion Ms. Cui Lanying passed by, he suddenly rushed out and stabbed Ms. Zhang's back and arms with the file three times, causing her to fall to the ground and cry for help. Ms. Cui grabbed his arm and shouted for the police, but she was also stabbed in the left arm. Police Officer No. 37 from Sandao Tou West Station arrived after hearing the alarm and chased after Tan, capturing him along with the murder weapon and taking him to the Huishan Police Station. He was sent to the First Special District Court for instructions pending the recovery of the victims. The two women were sent to the Tongren Hospital. Fortunately, the injuries were minor, and they were discharged from the hospital and returned home the next day. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan presided over a retrial at the Third Criminal Court. Public Works Department lawyer Li Zhishan presented the case. The two women then testified about the circumstances of the stabbing at the time. When questioned, the defendant's statement was evasive. Judge Wu sentenced Tan Dajinlong to eight months imprisonment and confiscated the file.

The Estranged Couple Cannot Reach an Agreement 162

Divorce Negotiations Fail

Disputes Over Living Expenses Arise Again

Lin Huantang, a Cantonese man, had a love affair with a Japanese woman after studying in the United States. They lived together for several years before bringing her to Shanghai, acting as husband and wife. However, he treated his original wife, Li Fenglin, as a stranger and did not provide for her. Ms. Li filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Court. The initial trial ruled that the two parties should live separately and that Lin should pay Ms. Li 60 yuan per month for living expenses. However, Lin claimed that he could not afford to pay and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court, requesting a reduction to 30 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Li, together with Judges Ye and Wu, held a hearing. After Lin's lawyer stated the intention of the appeal, Ms. Li's lawyer rebutted that Lin had married a Japanese woman and was living with her, so his monthly living expenses must be considerable. However, he claimed that he could not afford to pay his original wife 60 yuan per month for living expenses, which was clearly untrue. Lin's sole purpose was to get a divorce, but Ms. Li would accept it if there were appropriate terms. Therefore, they had negotiated outside once. Ms. Li initially wanted more than 5,000 yuan, but later reduced it to 5,000. Lin had gradually increased his offer to 4,400 yuan, which was not far off, and it was easy to reach an agreement. However, Lin broke his promise and reduced his offer to more than 3,000 yuan, which led to the breakdown of the negotiations. It was found that Lin's father owned a large amount of assets. Now that his father is dead, Lin has received more than 10,000 yuan of the inheritance. In addition, Lin brought 40,000 to 50,000 US dollars from the United States and had 5,000 in public bonds. He also had a house worth 30,000 yuan in his hometown, and also owned a house in the United States, which currently generates more than 20 US dollars in monthly rent. His claim that he only had several thousand in assets was purely a lie. Ms. Li also filed a counter-appeal, requesting that the living expenses be changed to 85 yuan per month and that Lin be ordered to provide a cash guarantee, etc. After the two parties concluded their arguments in court, the ruling was scheduled to be announced at 2:00 PM on the 12th of this month.

The Exchange Rate of Silver Dollars Rises Again 163

Yesterday's High Price Was 3,300 Wen

The local money industry opened yesterday, and the exchange rate of silver dollars rose sharply. Yesterday's high price was 330,000 wen for every 100 yuan in silver dollars, which is equivalent to 3,300 wen per silver dollar. The price of silver coins also rose, with one silver dollar exchanging for 12 silver coins and 369 wen. However, the exchange shops in the British and French Concessions and the Chinese areas of the North and South cities hung signs that they would only exchange 3,000 wen or 3,040-50 wen for each silver dollar, up to about 3,100 wen. The reason for this was that the exchange shops had lost too much on the copper coins and silver coins they had taken in last year.

Alcohol Explosion Causes House Collapse and Deaths on Xiamen Road 164

The House Collapsed First, Then Caught Fire, No One Escaped

Six People Severely Injured, Two Died From Their Injuries

丨Hidden Alcohol Found to be Used for Manufacturing Drugs丨

At No. 50 to 52 Xinglong, Lane 136 (Zunde Lane) south of the old Garbage Bridge at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Xiamen Road, the business has been open for many years. The house has six upper and six lower floors. Usually, goods resembling merchant's goods are brought in and out, so it is generally assumed to be a formal business, and no attention is paid to it. Yesterday was the fifth day of the abolished Lunar New Year, and all the shops opened in the early morning. Unexpectedly, at about 10:30 AM, a loud noise suddenly occurred in the lane, shocking the surrounding area. The nearby shops thought that a great disaster had befallen them, so they hurriedly closed their doors again. At the same time, the glass doors and windows of several shops were also shattered. For a time, there was a noisy uproar. After investigation, it was learned that the loud noise came from the Xinglong business. The entire house collapsed, and the walls of the neighboring Yufeng, Deyu Shenzhuang at No. 46, Hengsheng at No. 60, and the Jiading Textile Factory at No. 58 were all blown out. Before long, a fire suddenly broke out in the ruins of the Xinglong business, and the flames were raging and unapproachable. The lane watchman and the nearby patrolmen, hearing the alarm, immediately reported to the police station, which sent detectives to suppress and investigate. At the same time, the fire brigade dispatched fire trucks to extinguish the fire. It was then learned that all the men and women in the house had not escaped and were buried in the rubble. They quickly dug through the rubble and summoned ambulances to transport the injured to the hospital. It was not until around 12:00 PM that the fire was extinguished. At the same time, it was discovered that there were as many as eight casualties. ㈠ Tang Jijun, 28 years old, injured in both hands and feet. ㈡ Gao Guoqing, 39 years old, injured in the head and limbs. ㈢ Gao Tianji, 30 years old, injured in the shoulders and back. ㈣ Wang Yonggui, 31 years old, injured in the arms. ㈤ Shen Lindi, female, 15 years old, injured in both hands and shoulders. ㈥ Wan Wenxi, 28 years old, suffered the most severe burns all over his body and was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. There were also ㈦ and ㈧ two men, one about 20 years old and one about 30 years old, who died on the spot due to their injuries and were sent to the coroner's office for examination. Their names are unknown and are being investigated. As for the cause of the fire and the collapse of the house, after careful investigation by the police, it was learned that it was caused by the explosion of several large boxes of alcohol stored in the business. The reason why the business stored alcohol was very strange. The police repeatedly searched and found several pieces of drug-making equipment in the business, indicating that it was secretly engaged in illegal activities. Therefore, they are currently pursuing the main culprits and investigating the internal organization in order to bring them to justice.

Shanghai Municipal Council Approves Telephone Company's Revised Connection Contract 165

Previously, the Shanghai Telephone Company had established a connection contract with the Telephone Bureau, charging five cents for each call. Now, after mutual consultation, it has been agreed that for calls originating from the company's lines, the company will receive one-tenth of the phone fee, and for calls originating from the bureau's lines, the company will receive five percent of the phone fee. The company had submitted this matter to the Shanghai Municipal Council for approval. According to the review by the Director-General and the Head of the Finance Department of the Council, this solution is not disadvantageous to the Council or general users. The Board of Directors has therefore approved the contract with the Telephone Bureau according to the conditions presented by the company.

Additionally, the Telephone Company believes that the previous quarterly billing method was not very economical and often resulted in bad debt losses. They propose to switch to monthly advance payments starting from April 1st of this year, aligning with the practices elsewhere. The Shanghai Municipal Council has approved this request.

Scavenger Terrified by Two Corpses at Lonely Grave, Goes Mad 166

Male Corpse Found on Tomb with Blood Flowing All Over

Female Corpse Found Lying by Riverside, Features Unclear

丨Tragic Incident in the Countryside of Hongzhen, Zhabei丨

Behind Chenjiazhai, east of Hongzhen on Linping Road, Zhabei, there is a solitary grave, rarely passed by pedestrians on ordinary days. Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, a scavenger passing through the area suddenly discovered a male corpse lying on the grave, head pointing southeast and feet pointing northwest. The man was about twenty years old, wearing a gray twill long gown, with a black cotton robe underneath, a blue striped wool sweater, white long underwear, black cotton-padded trousers, white socks, and black shoes. Blood was flowing all over the ground beside him, a gruesome sight. Upon seeing this, the scavenger was greatly shocked and quickly ran away. However, near a small river to the left of the grave, he suddenly discovered another female corpse lying by the riverside. The woman was about thirty years old, wearing a black cloth shirt, with a red cotton-padded jacket underneath, black cotton trousers, and a white striped cloth undershirt. Her features were unclear, with bloodstains all over. In an instant, the scavenger encountered these two incidents, and his soul was shattered. He screamed in terror and ran, acting like a madman. After running about a li, he finally reached the Hongzhen sub-station and urgently reported to the station. After receiving the news, patrol officer Tang Guangwen immediately led the police to investigate. Indeed, they found two corpses lying there. They also observed that the male corpse had a gunshot wound on the right forehead, while the female corpse had five or six knife wounds on the left neck and face. Although they inquired widely among the neighboring villagers, no one recognized them. Therefore, it was difficult to determine when the incident occurred. After inspecting the surrounding traces, it seemed likely that they were murdered elsewhere and the bodies were moved to this location. They conducted another detailed inspection and prepared a report to be submitted to the Linping Road sub-bureau, which would then be forwarded to the main bureau. At the same time, they ordered the local bailiff to conduct a preliminary examination and investigate the identities of the deceased and the details of the case in order to apprehend the culprits.

Animal Epidemic Prevention Institute Establishes Swine Fever Prevention Experimental Zone 168

Planned to be Established First in Yinxiang District

The Animal Epidemic Prevention Institute, jointly operated by the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute of the Ministry of Industry, manufactures various animal epidemic serums and prophylactic bacterial liquids to prevent and control livestock diseases. They have sent personnel to the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway line to prevent and control swine fever, with considerable success. Provinces as far as Jiangxi, Sichuan, Guangxi, and Hebei have also placed orders for swine fever serum from the institute. In view of the importance of preventing swine fever in Shanghai, it is planned to divide the city into several districts for systematic prevention and control. The swine fever prevention experimental zone will be established first in Yinxiang. If livestock raised by residents in the zone develop infectious diseases, they can go to the institute for treatment. If preventive injections are needed, they will be completely free of charge.

Maid Suffers Abuse, Cries on the Street and is Rescued 169

Sent to the Child Welfare Association for Care

Zhao Mingyuan, who lives in Wutiaojie, Zhenjiang, married and had a daughter, whose childhood name was Lianzhen, who is twelve years old. He immediately prepared a document to send her to the sub-bureau, which then transferred her to the main bureau for relief. Rong Qiaolin Sues to Divide Her Maternal Grandfather's Estate 174

The late local detective of the French Concession Police, Gu Jisheng, ran real estate in Japan, accumulating more than 300,000 yuan. He owned a residence at 14 Pingjili Road and several rental properties. He married Chen, Guo, and Tan as concubines. Only Guo had three daughters, all of whom are married. Gu had no heirs, so in his later years, he adopted a son, named Wei Yi, who is now married and has children. Gu died of illness on the 13th day of the eighth lunar month of last year. All the property left behind was controlled by his adopted son, Wei Yi. Recently, Gu's great-granddaughter, Gao Rongqiaolin (35 years old this year, residing at 308 Boer Road, daughter of Gu's eldest daughter Genxiu, who married Rong Wenbin of Ningbo), claims that since her mother is deceased, she is legally entitled to inherit her maternal grandfather's estate. She claims that her maternal grandfather, Gu Jisheng, had a total estate of 348,000 yuan, and she requests that her uncle, Gu Wei Yi, allocate one-half to her. She hired a lawyer to send a letter to Gu Wei Yi, requesting a division, but Wei Yi ignored it. Gao Rongqiaolin hired Hu Jue as her agent and, based on the provisions of Articles 1138, 1140, and 1164 of the Civil Code, filed a complaint with the Civil Division of the Second Special Court, requesting a summons and a legal division. She also applied for litigation assistance because she could not afford the litigation fees. The court, based on the complaint, on the issue of litigation assistance, yesterday morning, Judge Li Liang summoned the plaintiff for questioning in Civil Court 7. Gao Rongqiaolin was represented by a lawyer, who stated the reasons why she could not afford the fees. The court then ordered a postponement to the 22nd of this month for further review.

Record of the Joint Meeting of the Rice Groups of the North and South Markets 176

The North and South City rice groups of the Shanghai Bean and Rice Trade Association held a joint meeting at 3:00 PM on the 7th at the Cuixiutang Hall of the Yu Garden in the city. More than 160 members attended, including Lu Jingwen, Yan Xiaoquan, Zhu Zixiang, Wu Rongsheng, Fu Qiangeng, and Wang Tianchou. After the meeting began as usual, Chairman Lu Jingwen reported the purpose of the meeting, briefly stating that since the establishment of our rice group last year, the achievements of the industry have been concrete and need not be elaborated. However, the commission is the main body of the business and should be discussed and decided. The commission should be in accordance with the existing regulations and should not be violated. If there is any trading done greedily or secretly, it will be punished for violating the industry regulations once discovered. The chairman proposed that he reluctantly serve as the group leader and, according to the agreed proposal, four departments should be established to cooperate and serve as the foundation of the rice group. Please discuss and decide. The four departments will be selected at the next meeting on the 20th, when the industry will be convened again for public recommendation. The outstanding balances of loans issued by the industry should be calculated in silver dollars, in accordance with the usual practice of various industries. Please decide publicly. It was decided that all outstanding balances collected by our industry should be in silver dollars and should not be reduced. It is stipulated that the store should pay foreign labor costs for sending money. This applies to cash. However, recently, stores often pay with term bills, which waste foreign labor costs. It seems that they can be cancelled. Please discuss the case and decide publicly. The foreign labor costs for term bills are cancelled. If cash is sent, the labor costs will still be paid according to the existing regulations. Whether there are any problems with the store accounts last year should be reported truthfully by the industry according to the regulations. Please do not conceal anything. It was decided that the association would notify the industry to report to the North and South offices within two days, and then review the measures. Zhu Geliangsheng of Shenli Bank reported that Xin Sheng Rice Store in Anqiao, Zhaoshi, owed more than 600 yuan in goods. Since the previous batch of goods had not been cleared, he came to apply for goods. If the goods are not continued to be allocated, he will use the excuse of donating to withhold the payment for the goods. Now it has been dragged over the New Year, and he still refuses to pay. It is difficult to reason with him. This meeting should be arranged to deal with the case. It was decided that if the store does have such behavior, do not trade with it according to the regulations. If there are still similar stores, they must also report to the North and South offices for review within two days. An industry report: Xi Zhenqing, the manager of Taixing Store, which went bankrupt last year, is now a shareholder and manager of Xin Tai Store. However, the manager bears joint and several liability. He should be dealt with according to the regulations. It was decided that since the manager of Xin Tai is Xi Zhenqing, the manager of Tai Xing, he will not be allowed to trade until the debts of Tai Xing are cleared. Also, if Shen Tongsheng, who buys goods, goes to the market to buy goods, he should also be dealt with according to the regulations and not be allowed to trade. All members of our industry should abide by this uniformly. Hu Wenan of Yishunjiu Bank reported that Shen Ruigen, who bought goods from Zhuang Hexing, which has gone bankrupt, has now opened Tongyu Rice Store west of the Laozha Bridge on Beijing Road and is also the manager. Should he be allowed to trade under the association's regulations? It was decided to suspend the transaction until he has cleared the debts of Zhuang Hexing, and then trade with him. Shi Shengbupu of Ruikang Bank reported that Gu Anbo, who bought goods from Yulong, has now formed Defeng Rice Store. Can he trade? It was decided that of course it would be difficult to trade with him until the debts of Yulong are cleared. Subsequently, Chen Taiqian, Xie Kangyong, and Shuntai reported that Yuansheng has not returned the payment for goods and has been dragging it on past the New Year. They also reported that Feng Shunyi, Yuanren, and others have paid with checks for the New Year. How should they be dealt with? It was decided to deal with it in the same way as the Xin Sheng case. The industry should report to the North and South offices and discuss the solutions together. It was decided that the industry would resume business on the tenth day of February.

Totaling 7.15 Million Yuan

It was calculated that District 6 was surveyed at the Shendang Town District Office, with 8,387 households, 19,013 large people, and 11,489 small people in disaster. The grades were divided using the words "Kang Funian Feng," with 382 "Kang" relief tickets, 3,318 "Fu" tickets, 3,826 "Nian" tickets, and 861 "Feng" tickets, for a total of 8,387 relief tickets. Relief clothing consisted of one jacket and one pair of trousers using the words "Nian Ci," for a total of 575 sets of relief clothing.
